My three favorite functionalities of Calendly are the ability to templatize the meeting type and length across the entire organization. Ease of access. Right? We have a tile in our SSO homepage. It sits in our Chrome bar.\n\nIt's integrated directly into our our Gmail.\n\nSo no matter where we are, we're just a few clicks and we can get that meeting booked.\n\nAnd then my probably top personal favorite is the ability to create one-off meetings where I can actually decide which available times I'm sharing with with the client or with the individual on my team.\n\nWe've estimated that we've saved nearly six hundred hours of time since implementing calendly. class="sc-dd2631d-0 jOxrUi"><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iiSnrV"><div height="auto" width="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 khFViT"><div data-testid="callout-banner" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 kcnDzS"><div data-testid="banner-items-cards" display="grid" width="100%" class="sc-a58b1cef-0 bzMVoP"><div direction="column" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 cteyFl"><div direction="column" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 kIYDKe"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24px" height="24px" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 cteyFl"><div direction="column" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 kIYDKe"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24px" height="24px" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 48 49"><path cteyFl"><div direction="column" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 kIYDKe"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24px" height="24px" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 48 49"><path class="sc-dd2631d-0 gvtZIj"><p font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 douCO">more meetings booked YOY</p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><h3 id="Challenges" class="sc-372af2a2-0 hihnyK">Challenges</h3><h5 font-weight="bold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 eivaRr">Immaculate care for customers and their data</h5><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">As a global provider of cybersecurity testing and consultation, HackerOne is dedicated to delivering the highest level of service while increasing their customers resistance to attack.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">For their Customer Success team, seamless scheduling is a top priority. The team relies on smooth digital meetings to drive HackerOnes growth, says Alek Relyea, Manager, Customer Success.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">To maintain our revenue and secure renewals, weve got to make sure our clients arent just happy, theyre successful. So, we live and breathe in Zoom, Alek says. Being able to quickly and easily schedule these meetings is absolutely crucial to our organization.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Various employees at HackerOne started using Calendly individually to set boundaries around their calendars and schedule meetings in just a few clicks.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">One of those employees using Calendly was Zander, Head of IT and Workplaces. When he and his colleagues started developing compliance policies for HackerOne, they realized theyd need to re-evaluate a large swath of the companys tech stack.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Zander says, We were quick to get HackerOne authorized for <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.iso.org/standard/27001" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 hTkEBj"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">ISO 27000</span></span></a></span>, <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.fedramp.gov/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 hTkEBj"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">FedRAMP</span></span></a></span>, and <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" href="https://www.aicpa-cima.com/topic/audit-assurance/audit-and-assurance-greater-than-soc-2" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 hTkEBj"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">SOC 2</span></span></a></span>. As a small company, that made us very proud. But it meant that we had to move and cut off certain applications.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Zander and his team had to investigate every app that the organization considered to make sure it was DPA and GDPR compliant, and CTPA certified. Even integrations within each tool had to be searched for potential gateways they might offer to malicious actors.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">During that vetting period, Calendly usage was put on hiatus while it went under the microscope. That left Alek and his team struggling to use other scheduling solutions.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">We tried using the scheduling automations attached to our sales email platform, but it was very clunky, Alek says.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">HackerOne soon swapped email tools: Unfortunately, the new email platform didnt have a scheduling tool at all.</p><div data-testid="callout-section" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jOxrUi"><div width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iiSnrV"><div data-testid="callout-rich-text" width="100%" height="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 gNa-DG"><span font-size="s28" font-weight="semiBold" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 edIMfl">"So we were stuck looking at our Google Calendar, seeing what was available, and manually typing emails to offer clients options, Alek says. It could take days or weeks to get a meeting scheduled. We were wasting an incredible amount of time going back and forth."</span></div></div></div><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">That lag time was impacting the critical meetings that HackerOnes experts relied on to advise their clients and keep up to date with their evolving needs.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Zander and his team worked diligently to weigh each apps business value against its security features.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">When it came to scheduling platforms, nothing compared to Calendly.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">We presented a couple of different options, but Calendly was the friendliest to our business. It had the best UX. It just really resonated with people, Zander says.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">HackerOne implemented <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 hTkEBj" href="/pricing"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Calendly for Enterprise</span></span></a></span> within the Customer Success team and it quickly spread through the product and management teams, as well.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">With nothing but Google Calendar and emails, it could take days or weeks to get a meeting scheduled, Alek says. We were wasting an incredible amount of time going back and forth.</p><h3 id="Solution" class="sc-372af2a2-0 hihnyK">Solution</h3><h5 font-weight="bold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 eivaRr">A flexible scheduling platform built for business</h5><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Alek was thrilled with Calendly right out of the gate. When we had our first enablement session with Calendly, I immediately thought, This is going to save us countless hours each week.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">He appreciated that Calendly was easy to learn. It let his team share their availability in just a few clicks, and book meetings in minutes.&nbsp;</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">It impressed him further that the people behind the solution seemed genuinely devoted to HackerOnes success.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">We had some feedback early on around the UI and we made some feature requests, Alek says. Those ideas were listened to, and many of them were implemented pretty quickly. To me, that proved it was a true partnership. As CSMs ourselves, we have pretty high standards for support.</p><figure width="auto" height="auto" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iMfKlp"><div direction="column" data-testid="video-player-wistia" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 XJtmH"><div width="auto" direction="column" data-testid="component-video-player" display="flex" class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-78c639b-0 jCLgiO ivIuXE"></div><div display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-78c639b-1 dYgRlu lJMtx"><div height="auto" width="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 eEXJEk"><div display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jbNABl"><div class="sc-a196fe79-0 dcfLXI wistia_responsive_wrapper" data-testid="wistia-embed" style="position:relative"><div class="wistia_video_foam_dummy" data-source-container-id="wistia-oi6dogfz3p-1" style="border: 0px; Having a template for each that we can share with the press of a button is really powerful, Alek says.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">As a manager, he relies on <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 hTkEBj" href="/blog/one-time-calendly-link"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">single-use links</span></span></a></span> to maximize his availability for his team while maintaining control of his schedule.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Alek says, My calendar is unbelievably full. So, I love to manually select which times I want to offer. It lets me spend more time enabling my team without getting slammed with ten meetings in one day.</p><h5 font-weight="bold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 eivaRr">Highly efficient processes</h5><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Calendlys integrations add extra speed to the scheduling process.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">We have a Calendly tile in our SSO homepage, an icon in our <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 hTkEBj" href="/blog/scheduling-chrome-extension"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Chrome bar</span></span></a></span>, and an integration directly in our <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 hTkEBj" href="/integration/calendly-for-chrome"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">Gmail</span></span></a></span>. So no matter where we are, we can get that meeting booked with just a few clicks, Alek says.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">These efficiencies have freed up time for HackerOne to implement other important projects, like setting up their new customer success software, Gainsight.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Calendly enabled us to implement Gainsight, and now we can automate touchpoints and gain data insights on our customer journey, Alek says. Its helping us make more informed decisions.</p><h5 font-weight="bold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 eivaRr">Safeguarding data with SSO and SCIM</h5><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">For HackerOne, <span class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 sc-9f52a7fd-0 MbaJp hCMKnR"><a data-testid="link-color-button" class="sc-3e7c06f7-0 sc-3e7c06f7-1 hTkEBj" href="/blog/enterprise-security-compliance"><span class="sc-3cc2ce94-0 gZgKOx"><span text-decoration="underline" class="sc-ed1f50a8-0 imAMjQ">security features</span></span></a></span> are essential.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Zander and his team trust Calendlys Okta SSO compatibility to reduce the vulnerability of having multiple login authentications.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">The number one threat against a companys data is people trying to log in as an employee into their applications and services, Zander says. Single sign-on (SSO) removes that risk.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Connecting all of HackerOnes applications through a single, secure funnel minimizes password management work by consolidating everything under one, strong credential.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Calendlys SCIM provisioning also lightens the load for IT. Calendly lets admins categorize users by department or function, and automate processes for creating and managing accounts.</p><h5 font-weight="bold" class="sc-372af2a2-0 eivaRr">Easy proof for compliance</h5><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Calendlys excellent documentation makes it easy for HackerOne to demonstrate compliance.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">Calendly goes above and beyond to publish their compliance information, Zander says. Thats important to us, because having an official document from a vendor is considered a more accurate source of truth by our auditors than just an email from their CSM.</p><p height="auto" font-weight="normal" class="sc-a4aa44fb-0 gPsCkV">With compliance-friendly security features and lightning-fast scheduling, Calendly is a perfect fit for HackerOne.</p><figure width="auto" height="auto" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 iMfKlp"><div direction="column" data-testid="video-player-wistia" display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 XJtmH"><div width="auto" direction="column" data-testid="component-video-player" display="flex" class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-78c639b-0 jCLgiO ivIuXE"></div><div display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 sc-78c639b-1 dYgRlu lJMtx"><div height="auto" width="100%" class="sc-fc49f4d0-0 eEXJEk"><div display="flex" width="100%" class="sc-dd2631d-0 jbNABl"><div class="sc-a196fe79-0 dcfLXI wistia_responsive_wrapper" data-testid="wistia-embed" style="position:relative"><div class="wistia_video_foam_dummy" data-source-container-id="wistia-d37qwn66ei-1" style="border: 0px;
